***дерьмо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дерьмо.html>дерьмо́</a> (4095)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерьмо.html>дерьмо́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">derʹmó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерьмо.html>дерьма́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shit, crap (excrement)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дерьмо.html>дерьмо́</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vot <b>derʹmó</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Oh, shit! (vulgar)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полный.html>по́лном</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дерьмо.html>дерьме́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v pólnom <b>derʹmé</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">up shit creek; in deep shit; screwed; fucked</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shit, crap (stuff, things)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> scumbag, shithead (a bad person)</li></ol>

***десант.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:десант.html>деса́нт</a> (10714)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">descente</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десант.html>деса́нт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">desánt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десант.html>деса́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десант.html>деса́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десант.html>деса́нтов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>landing <i>(of troops)</i></li>
<li>troops landed, landing party</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десант.html>деса́нт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">desánt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десантник.html>деса́нтник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">desántnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десантник.html>деса́нтника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десантник.html>деса́нтники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десантник.html>деса́нтников</a></b>)

***дескать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дескать.html>де́скать</a> (3305)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дескать.html>де́скать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">déskatʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>(<i>a particle to introduce direct speech, somebody else's words or thoughts - real or imaginary</i>), allegedly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>о́н</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дескать.html>де́скать</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́л</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ón, <b>déskatʹ</b>, ne znál.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He <b>says</b> he didn't know.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***деструктивный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:деструктивный.html>деструкти́вный</a> (30073)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">destruktiv</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деструктивный.html>деструкти́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">destruktívnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)деструкти́внее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)деструкти́вней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>destructive</li></ol>

***десятеро.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:десятеро.html>де́сятеро</a> (27806)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десятеро.html>де́сятеро</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">désjatero</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>ten (in a group together), ten of them
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:десятеро.html>де́сятеро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>дете́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>désjatero</b> detéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ten children</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:десятеро.html>де́сятеро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>désjatero</b> časóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ten watches</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:десятеро.html>де́сятеро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очко́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>désjatero</b> očkóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ten pairs of glasses</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:десятеро.html>де́сятеро</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>désjatero</b> iz nas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ten of us</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:десятеро.html>де́сятеро</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nas býlo <b>désjatero</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there were ten of us</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The nominative of a collective numeral governs the genitive plural of the noun, pronoun, or adjective. The other cases agree with that of the noun, pronoun, or adjective. Not used with feminine nouns. Used mostly when speaking of children and with a few nouns that are used in the plural only, such as <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очки́</a>, or with pronouns.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десятилетие.html>десятиле́тие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">desjatilétije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десятилетие.html>десятиле́тия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десятилетие.html>десятиле́тия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десятилетие.html>десятиле́тий</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:десяток.html>деся́ток</a> (748)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десяток.html>деся́ток</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">desjátok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десяток.html>деся́тка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десяток.html>деся́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десяток.html>деся́тков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ten, set of ten</li>
<li>tens, ten's place</li>
<li>decade</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dozens of, many</li></ol>

***десять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a> (403)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*desętь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*déḱm̥t</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ten</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">deci-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">désjatʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>ten (10)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">desjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative case and accusative case governs the genitive plural of the noun. In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>désjatʹ</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ten boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>десятью́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>desjatʹjú</b> málʹčikami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with ten boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>désjatʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately ten boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>désjatʹ</b> knig</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ten books</span></div></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li>10x, ten times as much

***деталь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:деталь.html>дета́ль</a> (2132)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">détail</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">détailler</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to set apart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Attested since the middle of 19th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деталь.html>дета́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">detálʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деталь.html>дета́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деталь.html>дета́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деталь.html>дета́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>detail, nicety</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> minutiae</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> part, component</li></ol>

***детектив.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:детектив.html>детекти́в</a> (8649)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детектив.html>детекти́в</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dɛtɛktív</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детектив.html>детекти́ва</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детектив.html>детекти́вы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детектив.html>детекти́вов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>detective</li>
<li>detective story (<i>book</i> or <i>film</i>), whodunit</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">person</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыщик.html>сы́щик</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sýščik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:следователь.html>сле́дователь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">slédovatelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оперативник.html>операти́вник</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">operatívnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">detective novel</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детективный.html>детекти́вный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:роман.html>рома́н</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dɛtɛktívnyj román</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***детский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тский</a> (888)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">déti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">détskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> child; child's, children's
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тская</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мната</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>détskaja</b> kómnata</i> ― <span class="e-translation">children's room</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">détskij dom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">children's home, orphanage</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тская</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:преступность.html>престу́пность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>détskaja</b> prestúpnostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">juvenile delinquency</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">child criminality</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сад.html>сад</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">détskij sad</i> ― <span class="e-translation">kindergarten</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">children's garden</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тская</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:площадка.html>площа́дка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">détskaja ploščádka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">playground</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">children's area</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:труд.html>труд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>détskij</b> trud</i> ― <span class="e-translation">child labor</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>childish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сад.html>сад</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial exclamation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>détskij</b> sad</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you are behaving like a child</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">kindergarten</span>”)</div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сад.html>сад</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:зачем.html>заче́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закрыть.html>закры́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кошка.html>ко́шку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шкаф.html>шкафу́</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Détskij</b> sad! Začém ty zakrýl kóšku v škafú?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">What a childish prank! What did you put the cat in the closet for?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> baby
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тская</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:коляска.html>коля́ска</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>détskaja</b> koljáska</i> ― <span class="e-translation">baby carriage, pram</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:детский.html>де́тское</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:питание.html>пита́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>détskoje</b> pitánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">baby food</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***деть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:деть.html>деть</a> (12978)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*děti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰeh₁-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">do</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деть.html>деть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">detʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:девать.html>дева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put, to place</li>
<li>to do with
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куда.html>куда́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:деть.html>деть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kudá <b>detʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">what to do with, how to spend</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to leave, to mislay
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куда.html>куда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очки́</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kudá ja <b>del</b> svoí očkí?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Where did I put my glasses?, What did I do with my glasses?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***деться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:деться.html>де́ться</a> (4088)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деть.html>деть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">detʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деться.html>де́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">détʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деваться.html>дева́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to disappear, to get (to another place)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куда.html>куда́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:делиться.html>де́лись</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очки́</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kudá <b>délisʹ</b> moí očkí?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Where did I put my glasses?, What did I do with my glasses?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to put oneself, to go away
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ла</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:куда.html>куда́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:деться.html>де́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стыд.html>стыда́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná ne znála, kudá <b>détʹsja</b> ot stydá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">She did not know where to put herself for embarrassment.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куда.html>куда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:деться.html>де́ться</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kudá mne <b>détʹsja</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Where shall I go? Where can I hide?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некуда.html>не́куда</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:деться.html>де́ться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nékuda <b>détʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is nowhere to go</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деть.html>деть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">detʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
